[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLibFuzzer with an XML dictionary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the XML parser reads past[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe end of a small heap allocation. The sanitizer log shows a [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m-byte read at an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddress immediately after a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte region, indicating a heap-buffer-overflow.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is classified as a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability, where a buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated via `xmlStrdup` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is read or copied beyond its allocated size.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash stack trace highlights these key frames:  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `__asan_memcpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe unsafe multi-byte copy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:4005[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlParseEntityValue` → `xmlParseEntityDecl` → `xmlParseInternalSubset` → [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseDocument` → `xmlCtxtParseDocument`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Fuzzer entry `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzz/xml.c`  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The buffer in question is allocated via `xmlStrndup`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`xmlStrdup` in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlFuzzMalloc`, representing an entity value string.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is triggered when expanding parameter entities [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during entity declaration parsing.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • AddressSanitizer identifies the redzone and reports the exact off-by-some-bytes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition: reading [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes from a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocation.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas to Investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand the full context, the following modules and functions should be [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreviewed:  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • parser.c around `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`, `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseEntityValue`, `xmlParseEntityDecl`, and `xmlParseInternalSubset`  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • entities.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlCreateEntity`, `xmlAddEntity`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and SAX2 handler in `SAX2.c`  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • xmlstring.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlStrndup`, `xmlStrdup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the custom allocator [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlFuzzMalloc`  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness in `fuzz/xml.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry point[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, though it is not the root [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese areas collectively handle entity declaration parsing and string buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement, which is where the overflow manifests.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m327[0m[39m:     * If there's enough space at the start of the buffer,[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m329[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m338[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > buf->maxSize - buf->use[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m769[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m770[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure that the buffer is double the necessary size[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m771[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This ensures no buffer overflow is possible[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m772[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m773[0m[39m:            return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m774[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m775[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m776[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m777[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m778[0m[39m:    buf->size += len;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m779[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap-buffer-overflow is triggered in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure because its [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgrowth logic only enlarges the buffer on the very first invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhen buf->cap [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. On any subsequent entity insertion, even if buf->cap − buf->size < len [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mi.e., not enough free space[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, no grow is performed and memcpy overruns the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: parser.c  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Function: static void [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlSBuf *buf, const xmlChar *str,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Outline  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Replace the one‐time‐only grow check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a capacity [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck identical in spirit to xmlSBufAddString:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Condition: if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap − buf->size <= len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → grow  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Grow amount: at least len [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor len*[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m to preserve doubling intent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Preserve the existing resource‐limit check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`buf->max − buf->size < len` → [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror code[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the final memcpy and size incrementation.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In parser.c, locate xmlSBufAddEntitySecure [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m762[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change this block:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure that the buffer is double the necessary size[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to something like:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure there is enough room for [0m[32m'len'[0m[39m more bytes[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size <= len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            unsigned growRequest = len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or len, to match doubling strategy[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, growRequest[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leave the resource‐limit guard above untouched.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change guarantees that before every memcpy into buf->mem, the buffer has [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeen grown sufficiently to hold the new data, closing the window for any overflow. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By mirroring the proven growth check from xmlSBufAddString, we maintain [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency across the codebase.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We keep the semantic of “secure” addition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., checking against buf->max[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintact.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The xmlSBufAddEntitySecure error code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on exceeding [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuf->max remains unchanged.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any outer logic that relies on buf->cap being zero to detect first‐time growth[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis unaffected, since buf->cap is set to nonzero by xmlSBufGrow and all subsequent [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations now correctly grow when needed.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other functions, harness code, tests, and utilities remain unmodified.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slightly more frequent reallocations may occur if many small entities are [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappended, but xmlSBufGrow’s doubling strategy will amortize that overhead.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new dependencies or API changes are introduced.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. References  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar grow‐when‐needed logic in xmlSBufAddString [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:782[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m792[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandles dynamic growth safely.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - xmlSBufGrow doubles buffer size, ensuring good amortized performance.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>parser.[0m[1;92mc:762[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m779[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4003[0m[39m:                [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Grow the buffer to handle the input[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4004[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, str - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:4003[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m4005[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code is invoking[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Here, `ent->name` is a string whose length is governed by the entity’s *name*,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut `ent->length` is the length of the *content*.  Passing `ent->length` as the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte‐count to copy from `ent->name` overruns the name buffer whenever the content [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis longer than the name.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All of the heap overflow reports occur in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure’s memcpy, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbecause it faithfully copies `len` bytes from a too‐small `str` buffer.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Strategy:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In parser.c’s xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue, change the source pointer passed to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure from `ent->name` to `ent->content`.  Since `ent->length` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindexes the content buffer, these two will now match and no out‐of‐bounds read will[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccur.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the improved growth‐condition logic in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevious patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  This ensures the *destination* buffer is grown to hold the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincoming bytes, but does *not* attempt to fix a mis‐sized *source* buffer.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Open src/libxml2/parser.c and locate xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue around line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4003[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Replace:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, str - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, str - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* copy the *content* [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot the name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Save and rebuild the library.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is a one‐line logical fix at the call‐site.  It addresses the true [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmismatch between source buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ent->name`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and length [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ent->length`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves all existing secure‐buffer logic, SAX‐handler wiring, and fuzzing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness unchanged.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It does not touch the fuzzer, harness code, or test suite.  All existing tests[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould still pass, and no external dependencies are modified.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m case that ent->content is NULL and ent->[0m[33mlength[0m[39m==[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL,[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is a no‐op [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno memcpy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, matching the previous [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior of passing name/[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m.  If ent->[0m[33mcontent[0m[39m==NULL but ent->length>[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, that [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates malformed entity data and will trigger either a null dereference or a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser error; this matches overall libxml2 error semantics.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code paths call xmlSBufAddEntitySecure with a mismatched [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer/length, so this patch is narrowly scoped.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Outcome:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After this change, AddressSanitizer can no longer observe a [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap‐buffer‐overflow in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure, because we only copy exactly the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumber of bytes actually allocated in `ent->content`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
